,KUN MKHYEN BLO BZANG GRAGS PA YAB SRAS SOGS, ,CHOS 'DI'I BRGYUD PA'I
BLA MA LHAR BCAS

MCHOD; ,THOS BSAM BSGOM PA'I GRU GZINGS LA BRTEN NAS, ,KUN MKHYEN
YE SHES RGYA MTSOR 'JUG 'DOD PA'I, ,DED DPON RNAMS LA THUB PA SANGS
RGYAS KYI, ,GO 'PHANG DGOS 'DOD KUN 'BYUNG 'DI RU ZHES, ,'JAM DPAL
DBYANGS KYI

GZHI; ,THUB BSTAN SPYI DANG KHYAD PAR TZONG KHA PA'I, ,BSTAN PA YIN
[*YUN] RING GNAS PA'I RGYU RU BSNGO, ,ZHES PA 'DI NI MKHAS DANG GRUB
PA KUN GYI GTZUG GI RGYAN DU GYUR NAS GNAM BSKOS 'JAM DBYANGS
GONG MA CHEN PO'I LUNG GIS STONG 'KHOR

SU, 'DZIN GRVA SO SOR

BSDUS TSAN RE GNYIS KHRID LTA BU MDZAD NAS GNANG BA'O, ,'DI'I NANG GI

SGRUB 'JUG BAR SKABS KYI TSIGS BCAD PHAL CHE MJUG RTZOM RNAMS KHA
SKONGS DANG BCAS TE ZHU

BA'I; ,'GRO TSOGS KUN LA BU GCIG LTAR BRTZE YAN LAG DRUG CU'I DBYANGS
LDAN GSUNG, ,'BRUG LTAR CHER SGROGS NYON MONGS GNYID SLONG LAS KYI
LCAGS SGROG 'GROL MDZAD CING, ,MA RIG MUN SEL SDUG BSNGAL MYU GU
JI SNYED

GCOD MDZAD RAL GRI BSNAMS, ,GDOD NAS DAG CING SA BCU'I MTHAR SON
YON TAN LHUN RDZOGS RGYAL SRAS THU BO'I SKU, ,BCU PHRAG BCU DANG
BCU GNYIS RGYAN SPRAS BDAG BLO'I MUN SEL 'JAM PA'I DBYANGS LA 'DUD,
